Expand the quadratic part:
\[
0.9909642091509507\,P\;-\;\frac{0.9909642091509507}{39.01184604772507}P^2\;+\;0.9909642091509507\,P^{1/3}\;+\;0.9909642091509507\,P
\]
So GT is exactly:
- a **\(P^2\)** term with coefficient \(-0.9909642091509507/39.01184604772507\) (negative),
- a **\(P\)** term with coefficient \(0.9909642091509507+0.9909642091509507=1.9819284183019014\),
- a **\(P^{1/3}\)** term with coefficient \(0.9909642091509507\),
- **no \(t\)** dependence, no logs/exp/tanh/etc.

Thus any matching candidate must be able (by parameter choice) to reduce to:
\[
aP^2 + bP + dP^{1/3}
\]
with the specific fixed \(a,b,d\) above, and with **no other functional dependence**.

### Candidate-by-candidate analysis

1. \(P^2(\cdots)+P(\cdots)+ P\frac{c3}{Pc4+1}+P c5\log(Pc6+1)+c7\tanh(\cdots)\)  
   Can kill tanh by \(c7=0\), kill log by \(c5=0\), kill rational by \(c3=0\). Then left with only \(P^2\) and \(P\) terms. **No way to create \(P^{1/3}\)**. Not match.

2. \(P^2 c0 + P^2 c1 e^{c2 t} + Pc3 + c4 t e^{c5 t}+c6\)  
   To remove \(t\): set \(c1=0\) or \(c2=0\) (but then still \(P^2\) ok), and set \(c4=0\). Also need \(c6=0\) (GT has no constant). Still only \(P^2\) and \(P\). **No \(P^{1/3}\)**. Not match.

3. Includes \(P c3\log(Pc4+c5)\) and tanh term. Set those coefficients to 0 to remove them → only \(P^2\) and \(P\). **No \(P^{1/3}\)**. Not match.

4. All terms are rational in \(t\) via \((c1+t)\). To remove \(t\)-dependence for all \(t\) you’d need all numerators 0 except possibly if expression becomes identically 0; but GT is not 0. Also no \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

5. Has \(P c2\log(Pc3+1)\), constant \(c4\), and \(t e^{c6 t}\). Can set \(c2=0,c4=0,c5=0\) to remove extras → only \(P^2\) and \(P\). **No \(P^{1/3}\)**. Not match.

6. Has \(P^{c4} c5 e^{c6 t}\). To remove \(t\), set \(c6=0\) so factor is constant; then you can choose \(c4=1/3\) and \(c5=0.990964...\) to match the \(P^{1/3}\) term. Also set \(c7=0\) to remove \(t e^{c8 t}\). Then remaining polynomial part is \(P^2 c0 + P(c1+c2+c3)\). This can match GT’s \(P^2\) and \(P\) coefficients by choosing \(c0\) and \(c1,c2,c3\) appropriately.  
   **This candidate can exactly represent \(aP^2+bP+dP^{1/3}\) with no \(t\)-dependence. Match is possible.**

7. Has \(P c2 (c3|P|)^{c4}\) which is \( \propto P|P|^{c4}\) giving \(P^{1+c4}\) for \(P>0\), and involves \(|P|\) (non-analytic sign issues) plus Max term. You could try to kill Max by \(c8=0\) and kill \(t\) term by \(c6=0\). But the power term is \(P^{1+c4}\), not \(P^{1/3}\) unless \(c4=-2/3\), which would introduce \(|P|^{-2/3}\) and yield \(P/|P|^{2/3}\), not equal to \(P^{1/3}\) for all real \(P\). Not match.

8. Has sine of log(|P|+1). Cannot become \(P^{1/3}\) for all \(P\). Can set sine coefficient 0, then no \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

9. Only \(P^2\) and \(P\) plus \(t\)-term and constant. Can remove \(t\) and constant, but **no \(P^{1/3}\)**. Not match.

10. Only polynomial in \(P\) plus \(t\)-dependent exp-of-sin. Kill that term → no \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

11. Has \(|P|\) and \(1/P^5\). Cannot equal \(P^{1/3}\) term; killing those removes needed term. Not match.

12. Has \(1/P^5\) and constant; no \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

13. Only \(P^2,P\) plus \(t\)-dependent exp(exp()). Kill \(t\) term → no \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

14. Has \(P c2 e^{Pc3}\) and rational \(P c5/(P+c6)\) and \(t\)-dependent exp. None can become \(P^{1/3}\) for all \(P\). Not match.

15. Has log(Pc8+1) multiplied by \(e^{c7 t}\). Kill it → no \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

16. Has \(P^2 c0 e^{c1 t}\) and \(P c3 e^{c4 t}\). To remove \(t\), set \(c1=0,c4=0,c6=0\). Then only \(P^2\) and \(P\). **No \(P^{1/3}\)**. Not match.

17. Has tanh and log*tanh. Kill them → only \(P^2\) and \(P\). No \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

18. Has \(P^{c4} c5 e^{c6 t}\) like candidate 6. Set \(c2=0\) (or \(c1=0\)) to remove \(t\) from \(P^2\) term, set \(c6=0\) to remove \(t\) from \(P^{c4}\) term, set \(c7=0\) to remove \(t e^{c8 t}\). Then expression becomes:
\[
P^2(\text{const}) + P(\text{const}) + c5 P^{c4}
\]
Choose \(c4=1/3\), \(c5=0.990964...\), and match \(P^2,P\) coefficients via remaining constants. **Match possible.**

19. Only \(P^2\) and \(P\) plus \(t\)-term. Kill \(t\)-term → no \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

20. Has \(P^{c4} c5 e^{c6 t}\) and tanh. Set \(c6=0\), \(c7=0\). Then can set \(c4=1/3\) and match coefficients as in 6/18. **Match possible.**

21. Has \(P^{c2}c3\sin(\cdot)\) which depends on \(t\) unless coefficient 0; if set to 0 then no \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

22. Only \(P^2,P\) plus \(t\)-dependent exp/tanh and constant. Kill extras → no \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

23. Has \(P\log(\cdot)\) and \(P e^{c5 t}\). Kill them → no \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

24. Has \(P^{c3}c4\) (good) but also Max term and \(t\)-term and constant. Set \(c5=0\) to remove \(t\)-term, set \(c7=0\) to remove Max, set \(c9=0\) to remove constant. Then:
\[
P^2 c0 + P(c1+c2) + c4 P^{c3}
\]
Choose \(c3=1/3\), \(c4=0.990964...\), and match \(P^2,P\) coefficients. **Match possible.**

25. Has \(P\cdot P^{c0}c1 = c1 P^{1+c0}\). Set \(c0=-2/3\) to get \(P^{1/3}\) term, but there are also \(P c2 + P c3\) (fine), plus \(t\)-term and \(e^{c7 t}\log(|P|+1)\). Kill those by \(c4=0\) and \(c6=0\). Then you have \(P^{1/3}\) and \(P\) but **no \(P^2\)** term at all. Not match.

26. Only \(P^2,P\) and \(P\log\) terms plus \(t\)-term. Kill logs and \(t\) → no \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

27. Only \(P^2,P\) plus rational \(P/(Pc4+1)\) and tanh. Kill extras → no \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

28. Similar: only \(P^2,P\) plus rationals and tanh. No \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

29. Has \(P c2 e^{Pc3}\) and \(P c5 e^{c6 t}\) and \(t\)-dependent exp. No way to get pure \(P^{1/3}\) for all \(P\). Not match.

30. Only \(P^2\) and \(P\) plus \(t\)-term. No \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

31. Only \(P^2,P\) plus rational and \(P e^{c6 t}\) and tanh. If kill \(t\) and extras → no \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

32. Has \(P c1 e^{Pc2}\) and log term. Not convertible to \(P^{1/3}\) for all \(P\). Not match.

33. Only \(P^2,P\) plus \(t\)-term. No \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

34. Has \(P c4 e^{P c5}\). Not \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

35. Has \(P e^{c5 t}\log(Pc6+1)\). Not \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

36. Has \(P\log(c3/|P|+1)\) and \(1/P^5\). Not \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

37. Has \(P\log(c5/(P+c6)+1)\). Not \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

38. Only \(P^2,P\) plus \(t\)-dependent exp. No \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

39. Has \(P^{c1}c2\log(Pc3+1)\) and Max. Not \(P^{1/3}\) polynomial term. Not match.

40. Only \(P^2,P\) plus \(t\)-dependent exp and constant. No \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

41. Has \(P\cdot \text{Max}(0,Pc5+1)\) (piecewise). Cannot equal smooth \(P^{1/3}\) term. Not match.

42. Only \(P^2,P\) plus rational and tanh and constant. No \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

43. Only \(P^2,P\) plus rational and \(t\)-dependent exp and constant. No \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

44. Only \(P^2,P\) plus \(t\)-dependent exp and \(1/(c8 t+1)^5\). No \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

45. Only \(P^2,P\) plus tanh and constant. No \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

46. Only \(P^2,P\) plus tanh. No \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

47. Only \(P^2,P\) plus \(t\)-dependent exp. No \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

48. Has \(P\cdot (Pc3)^{c4} = c3^{c4} P^{1+c4}\). Set \(c4=-2/3\) to get \(P^{1/3}\). Also has \(P^2\) term and linear \(P\) terms; tanh can be killed by setting its coefficient 0. Then you can match \(P^2\), \(P\), and \(P^{1/3}\) coefficients by choosing constants appropriately. **Match possible.**

49. Only \(P^2,P\) plus tanh. No \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

50. Only \(P^2,P\) plus tanh and \(1/P^5\). No \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.
